<div>   
<p style=";font-size: 14px;font-family: DengXian;white-space: normal;background: white"><br></p><p style="margin: 0 0 10px;font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;white-space: normal;text-indent: 25px;line-height: 25px;background: white"><span style="font-family: "times new roman";"><span style="font-family: "Times New Roman", serif; color: #3333FF;">2020</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">年度</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-family: "Times New Roman", serif; color: #3333FF;">JCR</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">共收录科技期刊</span><span style="font-family: "Times New Roman", serif; color: #3333FF;">9500</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">种，相比</span><span style="font-family: "Times New Roman", serif; color: #3333FF;">2019</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">年度的</span><span style="font-family: "Times New Roman", serif; color: #3333FF;">9370</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">种增加</span><span style="font-family: "Times New Roman", serif; color: #3333FF;">130</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">种，增幅为</span><span style="font-family: "Times New Roman", serif; color: #3333FF;">1.37%</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">。</span></span></span></p><p style="margin: 0 0 10px;font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;white-space: normal;text-indent: 25px;line-height: 25px;background: white"><span style="font-family: "times new roman";"><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">本年度中国大陆地区（</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-family: "Times New Roman", serif; color: #3333FF;">China Mainland</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">）计有</span><span style="font-family: "Times New Roman", serif; color: #3333FF;">252</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">种期刊被收录，相比</span><span style="font-family: "Times New Roman", serif; color: #3333FF;">2019</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">年度的</span><span style="font-family: "Times New Roman", serif; color: #3333FF;">241</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">种增加</span><span style="font-family: "Times New Roman", serif; color: #3333FF;">11</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">种，增幅为</span><span style="font-family: "Times New Roman", serif; color: #3333FF;">4.56%</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">。</span></span></span></p><p style="margin: 0 0 10px;font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;white-space: normal;text-indent: 25px;line-height: 25px;background: white;overflow-wrap: break-word"><span style="font-family: "times new roman";"><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">从影响因子的学科分区看，</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-family: "Times New Roman", serif; color: #3333FF;">2020</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">年度中国大陆地区期刊位列</span><span style="font-family: "Times New Roman", serif; color: #3333FF;">Q1</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">区</span><span style="font-family: "Times New Roman", serif; color: #3333FF;">(“</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">期刊影响因子的学科相对排名</span><span style="font-family: "Times New Roman", serif; color: #3333FF;">”</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">的分值为</span><span style="font-family: "Times New Roman", serif; color: #3333FF;">75.0—100)</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">的期刊数量相对</span><span style="font-family: "Times New Roman", serif; color: #3333FF;">2019</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">年度的</span><span style="font-family: "Times New Roman", serif; color: #3333FF;">74</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">种上升至</span><span style="font-family: "Times New Roman", serif; color: #3333FF;">85</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">种，占总数</span><span style="font-family: "Times New Roman", serif; color: #3333FF;">252</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">种的</span><span style="font-family: "Times New Roman", serif; color: #3333FF;">33.7%</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">，</span><span style="font-family: "Times New Roman", serif; color: #3333FF;">Q2</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">区</span><span style="font-family: "Times New Roman", serif; color: #3333FF;">(</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">影响因子的学科相对排名为</span><span style="font-family: "Times New Roman", serif; color: #3333FF;">50.0—75.0)</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">期刊</span><span style="font-family: "Times New Roman", serif; color: #3333FF;">76</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">种，占总数</span><span style="font-family: "Times New Roman", serif; color: #3333FF;">252</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">种的</span><span style="font-family: "Times New Roman", serif; color: #3333FF;">30.2%</span><span style="font-family: "times new roman"; color: #3333FF;">。</span></span></span></p><p style="margin: 0 0 10px;font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;white-space: normal;text-indent: 25px;line-height: 25px;background: white;overflow-wrap: break-word"><span style="font-family: "times new roman";"><strong style="text-align: center; text-indent: 24px;"><br></strong></span></p><p style="margin: 0 0 10px;font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;white-space: normal;text-indent: 25px;line-height: 25px;background: white;overflow-wrap: break-word"><strong style="text-align: center;
